Similarly to the book, we can introduce equational reasoning in agda.
I'm using the definitions from the [agda-stdlib](https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.Core.html#2708).

## Section 2.4 Homotopies and equivalences

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_∼_"></a><a id="5827" href="Chapter2.Book.html#5827" class="Function Operator">_∼_</a> <a id="5831" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5833" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5834" href="Chapter2.Book.html#5834" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="5836" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5838" href="Chapter1.Book.html#345" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="5840" href="Chapter1.Book.html#328" class="Generalizable">𝒾</a><a id="5841" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5843" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5844" href="Chapter2.Book.html#5844" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="5846" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5848" href="Chapter2.Book.html#5834" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="5850" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5852" href="Chapter1.Book.html#345" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="5854" href="Chapter1.Book.html#330" class="Generalizable">𝒿</a><a id="5855" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5857" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5859" href="Chapter1.Book.html#743" class="Function">Π</a> <a id="5861" href="Chapter2.Book.html#5844" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="5863" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5865" href="Chapter1.Book.html#743" class="Function">Π</a> <a id="5867" href="Chapter2.Book.html#5844" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="5869" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5871" href="Chapter1.Book.html#345" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="5873" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5874" href="Chapter1.Book.html#328" class="Generalizable">𝒾</a> <a id="5876" href="Agda.Primitive.html#961" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5878" href="Chapter1.Book.html#330" class="Generalizable">𝒿</a><a id="5879" class="Symbol">)</a>

## 2.7 Σ-types

I'm using a slightly different definition of the `f` in the following
theorem, as it'll be useful further on.

## 2.9 Π-types and the function extensionality axiom

## 2.10 Universes and the univalence axiom

## 2.11 Identity type

<pre class="Agda"><a id="21875" class="Comment">-- Lemma 2.11.1.</a>
<a id="isEquiv⇒isEquiv-ap"></a><a id="21892" href="Chapter2.Book.html#21892" class="Function">isEquiv⇒isEquiv-ap</a> <a id="21911" class="Symbol">:</a>

           <a id="21957" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21959" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="21960" href="Chapter2.Book.html#21960" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="21962" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="21964" href="Chapter2.Book.html#21927" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="21966" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21968" href="Chapter2.Book.html#21937" class="Bound">B</a><a id="21969" class="Symbol">)</a>
           <a id="21982" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="21984" href="Chapter2.Book.html#8094" class="Function">isEquiv</a> <a id="21992" href="Chapter2.Book.html#21960" class="Bound">f</a>

    <a id="33952" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33952" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="33958" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33960" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33961" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33961" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="33963" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="33965" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33821" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33967" href="Chapter1.Book.html#4615" class="Function Operator">≡</a> <a id="33969" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33823" class="Bound">B</a><a id="33970" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33972" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="33974" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33975" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33821" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="33977" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33979" href="Chapter2.Book.html#9938" class="Function">≃-refl</a> <a id="33986" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33821" class="Bound">A</a><a id="33987" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="33989" href="Chapter1.Book.html#4615" class="Function Operator">≡</a> <a id="33991" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="33992" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33823" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="33994" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="33996" href="Chapter2.Book.html#8871" class="Function">≃-→</a> <a id="34000" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34001" href="Chapter2.Book.html#17487" class="Function">≡-𝒰-≃</a> <a id="34007" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33821" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34009" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33823" class="Bound">B</a><a id="34010" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34012" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33961" class="Bound">p</a><a id="34013" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="34019" href="Chapter2.Book.html#33952" class="Function">lemma</a> <a id="34025" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34026" href="Chapter1.Book.html#4575" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="34031" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34031" class="Bound">A</a><a id="34032" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34034" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="34036" href="Chapter2.Book.html#13397" class="Function">pair⁼</a><a id="34041" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34042" href="Chapter1.Book.html#4575" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="34047" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="34049" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34051" href="Chapter1.Book.html#4575" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="34056" class="Symbol">_)</a>
</pre>
Also `×` is commutative in the following sense
<pre class="Agda"><a id="×-comm"></a><a id="34119" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34119" class="Function">×-comm</a> <a id="34126" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34128" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34129" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34129" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34131" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34133" href="Chapter1.Book.html#345" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="34135" href="Chapter1.Book.html#328" class="Generalizable">𝒾</a><a id="34136" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34138" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34139" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34139" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="34141" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34143" href="Chapter1.Book.html#345" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="34145" href="Chapter1.Book.html#330" class="Generalizable">𝒿</a><a id="34146" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34148" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34150" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34129" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34152" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1752" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="34154" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34139" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="34156" href="Chapter2.Book.html#8754" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="34158" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34139" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="34160" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1752" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="34162" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34129" class="Bound">A</a>

 <a id="34216" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="34224" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34224" class="Function">map</a> <a id="34228" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="34230" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="34232" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34233" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34233" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="34235" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34237" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34237" class="Bound">y</a><a id="34238" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34240" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34242" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34243" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34237" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="34245" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34247" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34233" class="Bound">x</a><a id="34248" class="Symbol">)</a>

          <a id="34438" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34440" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34441" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="34443" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34443" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="34445" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="34447" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34395" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34449" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">,</a> <a id="34451" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34405" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="34453" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34443" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="34455" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1752" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="34457" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34419" class="Bound">Q</a><a id="34458" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34460" href="Chapter2.Book.html#8754" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="34462" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="34464" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="34466" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34466" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="34468" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="34470" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34395" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34472" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">,</a> <a id="34474" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34405" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="34476" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34466" class="Bound">x</a><a id="34477" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34479" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1752" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="34481" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34419" class="Bound">Q</a><a id="34482" class="Symbol">)</a>

 <a id="34541" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="34549" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34549" class="Function">map</a> <a id="34553" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="34555" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="34557" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34558" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34558" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="34560" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34562" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34562" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="34564" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34566" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34566" class="Bound">z</a><a id="34567" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34569" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34571" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="34573" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34558" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="34575" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34577" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34562" class="Bound">y</a><a id="34578" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34580" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34582" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34566" class="Bound">z</a><a id="34583" class="Symbol">)</a>

`Σ` commutes with itself in the sense that
<pre class="Agda"><a id="Σ-comm"></a><a id="34703" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34703" class="Function">Σ-comm</a> <a id="34710" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34712" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="34713" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34713" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34715" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34717" href="Chapter1.Book.html#345" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="34719" href="Chapter1.Book.html#328" class="Generalizable">𝒾</a><a id="34720" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="34722" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="34723" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34723" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="34725" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34727" href="Chapter1.Book.html#345" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="34729" href="Chapter1.Book.html#330" class="Generalizable">𝒿</a><a id="34730" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="34732" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34733" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34733" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="34735" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="34737" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34713" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34739" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34741" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34723" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="34743" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34745" href="Chapter1.Book.html#345" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="34747" href="Chapter1.Book.html#332" class="Generalizable">𝓀</a><a id="34748" class="Symbol">)</a>
       <a id="34757" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34759" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34760" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="34762" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34762" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="34764" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="34766" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34713" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34768" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">,</a> <a id="34770" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="34772" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34772" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="34774" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="34776" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34723" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="34778" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">,</a> <a id="34780" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34733" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="34782" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34762" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="34784" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34772" class="Bound">y</a><a id="34785" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34787" href="Chapter2.Book.html#8754" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="34789" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34790" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="34792" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34792" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="34794" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="34796" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34723" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="34798" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">,</a> <a id="34800" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="34802" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34802" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="34804" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="34806" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34713" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="34808" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1647" class="Function">,</a> <a id="34810" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34733" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="34812" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34802" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="34814" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34792" class="Bound">y</a><a id="34815" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="34817" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34703" class="Function">Σ-comm</a> <a id="34824" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34824" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="34826" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="34828" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34875" class="Function">map</a> <a id="34832" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34834" href="Chapter2.Book.html#8266" class="Function">invs⇒equivs</a> <a id="34846" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34875" class="Function">map</a> <a id="34850" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34851" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34911" class="Function">map⁻¹</a> <a id="34857" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34859" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34949" class="Function">ε</a> <a id="34861" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34863" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34960" class="Function">η</a><a id="34864" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="34867" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="34875" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34875" class="Function">map</a> <a id="34879" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="34881" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="34883" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34884" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34884" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="34886" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34888" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34888" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="34890" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34892" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34892" class="Bound">z</a><a id="34893" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34895" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34897" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34898" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34888" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="34900" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34902" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34884" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="34904" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34906" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34892" class="Bound">z</a><a id="34907" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="34911" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34911" class="Function">map⁻¹</a> <a id="34917" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="34919" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="34921" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34922" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34922" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="34924" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34926" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34926" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="34928" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34930" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34930" class="Bound">z</a><a id="34931" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="34933" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="34935" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="34936" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34926" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="34938" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34940" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34922" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="34942" href="Chapter1.Book.html#1598" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="34944" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34930" class="Bound">z</a><a id="34945" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="34949" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34949" class="Function">ε</a> <a id="34951" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="34953" href="Chapter1.Book.html#4575" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
  <a id="34960" href="Chapter2.Book.html#34960" class="Function">η</a> <a id="34962" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="34964" href="Chapter1.Book.html#4575" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a>
</pre>
Since we don't have cumulativity we'll use the fact that `raise` is a equivalence.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="raise⁻¹"></a><a id="35066" href="Chapter2.Book.html#35066" class="Function">raise⁻¹</a> <a id="35074" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35076" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35077" href="Chapter2.Book.html#35077" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="35079" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35081" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="35086" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35088" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35089" href="Chapter2.Book.html#35089" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="35091" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35093" href="Chapter1.Book.html#345" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="35095" href="Chapter1.Book.html#328" class="Generalizable">𝒾</a><a id="35096" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35098" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="35100" href="Chapter1.Book.html#617" class="Datatype">Raised</a> <a id="35107" href="Chapter2.Book.html#35077" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="35109" href="Chapter2.Book.html#35089" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="35111" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="35113" href="Chapter2.Book.html#35089" class="Bound">A</a>
<a id="35115" href="Chapter2.Book.html#35066" class="Function">raise⁻¹</a> <a id="35123" href="Chapter2.Book.html#35123" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="35125" href="Chapter2.Book.html#35125" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="35127" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35128" href="Chapter1.Book.html#666" class="InductiveConstructor">raise</a> <a id="35134" href="Chapter2.Book.html#35134" class="Bound">x</a><a id="35135" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35137" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="35139" href="Chapter2.Book.html#35134" class="Bound">x</a>

<a id="≡-Raised-≃"></a><a id="35142" href="Chapter2.Book.html#35142" class="Function">≡-Raised-≃</a> <a id="35153" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35155" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35156" href="Chapter2.Book.html#35156" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="35158" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35160" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="35165" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35167" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35168" href="Chapter2.Book.html#35168" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="35170" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35172" href="Chapter1.Book.html#345" class="Function">𝒰</a> <a id="35174" href="Chapter1.Book.html#328" class="Generalizable">𝒾</a><a id="35175" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35177" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="35179" href="Chapter1.Book.html#617" class="Datatype">Raised</a> <a id="35186" href="Chapter2.Book.html#35156" class="Bound">𝒿</a> <a id="35188" href="Chapter2.Book.html#35168" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="35190" href="Chapter2.Book.html#8754" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="35192" href="Chapter2.Book.html#35168" class="Bound">A</a>
